msg:When traveling to Shanxi, it will be more comfortable if you let go of your obsession with Beijing, Shanghai and Guangzhou. Generally speaking, people in Shanxi have nothing to do. They are neither treacherous nor slippery, but they really don't like to work. This lack of diligence is reflected in the lack of details. On the whole, they look pretty good. Datong Hotel is an old state-owned hotel. The hardware is guaranteed, but there are no details. Our room was basically not cleaned, but the towels and mineral water were still changed for you. When you go swimming in the swimming pool, your aunt wants you to come in your swimsuit and leave wet. But she sees that you are really unprepared, so she takes out a locker key and gives it to you. When traveling in Shanxi this time, I found that this is a normal behavior of Shanxi people, that is, if they can do less, they will still be happy to help you if it is really inconvenient for you. If you understand this, you won't be too picky about Shanxi hotels. Just find one with complete hardware facilities and no software.

On the 1st, I came back after eating more than 8 o'clock in the evening. My wife remixed in the elevator hall on the 5th floor and couldn't get up for a long time. At that time, the hall was dim and there were no lights, and there was a dark slope at the junction of the carpet and the ground (the carpet collapsed over time), which made it easy to trip. After calling and waiting for a long time, an on-duty manager came. I took it to the emergency depar**ent of Datong No. 3 Hospital. It showed that my right shoulder and arm were not broken, but it was painful when I moved. The pain did not relieve the next day, and I still couldn't move. I tried to find a local specialized orthopedist but couldn't find it. Decided to return to Beijing for inspection on the 3rd in the morning. Before leaving the hotel, a manager surnamed Cao came to talk, saying that the hotel can only waive the room fee, but nothing else. After returning to Beijing, the medical expenses and lost work expenses do not matter, and both parties are responsible for it. Seeing that the other party was impatient and insincere, he decided not to delay any further time, nor did he accept their free room charge. It is worth mentioning that Ctrip has always been professional and patient in the process. The manager called many times to ask about the situation, communicated and followed up, and made some compensation on the road, which is comforting. But this old hotel that is in charge has no phone calls, no information, no results.
